INTRODUCTION_NNP ._.
Dairy_NN cows_NNS depend_VBP upon_JJ roughages_NNS as_IN the_DT principal_JJ natural_JJ sources_NNS of_IN calcium_NN ,_, and_CC upon_IN grains_NNS and_CC milling_VBG by-products_NNS for_IN most_JJS of_IN the_DT phosphorus_NN ._.
Grasses_NNS provide_VBP from_IN one-fifth_JJ to_TO one-third_JJ as_IN much_JJ calcium_NN ,_, and_CC about_RB three-fifths_NNS as_IN much_JJ phosphorus_NN as_IN do_VBP the_DT legumes_NNS grown_VBN under_IN the_DT same_JJ conditions_NNS ._.
The_DT calcium_NN content_NN of_IN the_DT forages_NNS grown_VBN on_IN low-lime_JJ soils_NNS is_VBZ lower_JJR than_IN that_DT of_IN the_DT same_JJ kinds_NNS of_IN plants_NNS on_IN more_JJR fertile_JJ soils_NNS ._.
Lactating_VBG cows_NNS dependent_NN on_IN grass_NN forages_NNS grown_VBN on_IN low-lime_JJ soils_NNS often_RB deplete_VBP their_PRP$ reserves_NNS of_IN calcium_NN to_TO such_PDT an_DT extent_NN that_IN skeletal_JJ strength_NN and_CC yield_NN of_IN milk_NN are_VBP affected_VBN ._.
STATEMENT_NNP OF_NNP PROBLEM_NNP ._.
The_DT Jersey_NNP cows_NNS in_IN the_DT Florida_NNP Agricultural_NNP Experiment_NNP Station_NNP dairy_NN herd_NN were_VBD dependent_JJ upon_IN pasture_NN grasses_NNS ,_, and_CC corn_NN or_CC sorghum_NN silages_NNS ,_, as_IN the_DT main_JJ sources_NNS of_IN roughages_NNS ._.
Since_IN December_NNP ,_, 1920_CD ,_, alfalfa_FW meal_NN was_VBD included_VBN as_IN one-ninth_JJ to_TO one-eighth_NN of_IN the_DT concentrates_NNS mentioned_VBN in_IN the_DT herd_NN records_NNS and_CC annual_JJ reports_NNS of_IN the_DT station_NN ._.
One_CD cow170_VBZ THE_DT INDIAN_NNP JOURNAL_NNP OF_NNP VETERINARY_NNP SCIENCE_NNP AND_NNP ANIMAL_NNP HUSBANDRY_NNP [_NNP IV_NNP ,_, II_NNP ._.
REVIEW_NNP OF_NNP LITERATURE_NNP ._.
Eckles_NNS (_( 2_CD )_) observed_VBD that_IN cows_NNS on_IN phosphorus-deficient_JJ rations_NNS produced_VBD much_RB less_JJR milk_NN than_IN when_WRB the_DT lacking_VBG mineral_NN was_VBD supplied_VBN ._.

Fingerling_NNP (_( 3_CD )_) obtained_VBD similar_JJ results_NNS with_IN milk_NN goats_NNS on_IN rations_NNS the_DT basal_JJ portion_NN of_IN which_WDT was_VBD deficient_NN in_IN calcium_NN ._.
Meigs_NNP and_CC Woodward_NNP (_( 5_CD )_) con-_NN cluded_VBD that_IN cows_NNS produced_VBD appreciably_RB more_RBR milk_NN after_IN having_VBG been_VBN placed_VBN in_IN good_JJ mineral_JJ storage_NN during_IN the_DT preceding_VBG dry_JJ period_NN ._.
Kellner_NNP (_( 4_CD )_) mentioned_VBD that_IN dairy_NN rations_NNS are_VBP deficient_JJ in_IN calcium_NN more_RBR fre-_JJ quently_RB than_IN they_PRP are_VBP in_IN phosphorus_NN ._.
Under_IN these_DT conditions_NNS ,_, cows_NNS withdraw_VBP mineral_JJ matter_NN from_IN the_DT bones_NNS in_IN order_NN to_TO maintain_VB milk_NN production_NN ._.
As_IN this_DT impoverishment_NN progresses_VBZ ,_, the_DT milk_NN yield_NN is_VBZ decreased_VBN ._.
Nessler_NNP (_( 6_CD )_) found_VBD that_IN the_DT bones_NNS of_IN a_DT cow_NN affected_VBN with_IN Knochenbruchigkeit_NNP (_( bone-fragility_NN )_) contained_VBD less_JJR calcium_NN and_CC phosphorus_NN ,_, were_VBD lighter_RB in_IN weight_NN ,_, and_CC had_VBD thinner_NN shaft_NN walls_NNS than_IN had_VBD those_DT of_IN a_DT healthy_JJ cow_NN ._.
The_DT spongy_JJ bonesEFFECT_NN OF_IN CALCIUM-DEFICIENT_NNP ROUGHAGES_NNP 171_CD were_VBD eliminated_VBN from_IN the_DT station_NN herd_NN ,_, and_CC bone_RB strengths_NNS determined_VBD similarly_RB ,_, using_VBG a_DT 6-inch_JJ span_NN ._.
Similar_JJ data_NNS were_VBD obtained_VBN from_IN the_DT leg_JJ bones_NNS of_IN three_CD range_NN cows_NNS ,_, six_CD Aberdeen_NNP Angus_NNP cows_NNS and_CC 24_CD three-year_JJ old_JJ steers_NNS ._.

The_DT pyrethrum_NN plant_NN belongs_NNS to_TO the_DT genus_NN Chrysanthemum_NNP ,_, of_IN the_DT family_NN Com-_NNP positae_NN ._.

The_DT term_NN pyrethrum_NN refers_NNS to_TO the_DT entire_JJ plant_NN ,_, while_IN pyrethrin_NN designates_VBZ only_RB the_DT active_JJ principle_NN ._.
Within_IN recent_JJ years_NNS ,_, pyrethrum_NN has_VBZ become_VBN one_CD of_IN our_PRP$ most_RBS valuable_JJ insecticides_NNS and_CC large_JJ quantities_NNS of_IN the_DT flowers_NNS are_VBP imported_VBN annually_RB into_IN this_DT country_NN from_IN Japan_NNP ,_, Italy_NNP and_CC other_JJ countries_NNS where_WRB this_DT plant_NN is_VBZ cultivated_VBN ._.
